[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA SEGV [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSegmentation Fault[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m crash has been detected in the Wireshark codebase [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing of the BAT [0m[1;39m([0m[39mB.A.T.M.A.N.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m VIS protocol dissector. The crash occurs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function at line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m of `packet-bat.c`, triggered by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man invalid memory read at address `[0m[1;36m0x202020a0030c28[0m[39m`. The AddressSanitizer reports [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis as a wild address read with a scariness score of [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m, indicating a potentially [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexploitable vulnerability involving format string specifiers in the crafted input.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as an AddressSanitizer SEGV error during the execution of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`handler_bat.vis` fuzzer with libFuzzer as the fuzzing engine. The crash is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered when processing a specially crafted test case designed to test the BAT [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVIS protocol dissector.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Type:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash appears to be related to a format string vulnerability combined with an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid memory access. The input data contains multiple format string specifiers [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`%x`, `%n`, `%s`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that are being processed by `fprintf_chk` and related printf [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfamily functions, suggesting that user-controlled input may be improperly used as a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat string.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Observations:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Crash Location**: The error originates in `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-bat.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m`, which calls `fprintf_chk` with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially malicious format strings.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Access Pattern**: The invalid read at address `[0m[1;36m0x202020a0030c28[0m[39m` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggests an attempt to access memory at an address that appears to be constructed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe pattern `[0m[1;36m0x20[0m[39m` repeated multiple times may correspond to space [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters in the input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Input Characteristics**: The hex dump of the triggering input reveals:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple format string specifiers: `%x` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhexadecimal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `%n` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwrite number of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `%s` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstring[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Repeated patterns of [0m[32m'X'[0m[39m and [0m[32m'A'[0m[39m characters[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The string [0m[32m"IXXXX.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%x.%n.%s"[0m[39m followed by padding[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis**: The crash occurs through the following path:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_bat_vis` → `dissect_bat_vis_v24` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Format string processing via `__fprintf_chk` → `vfprintf` → `printf_common`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory access check in `QuickCheckForUnpoisonedRegion`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **DEDUP Token**: `QuickCheckForUnpoisonedRegion--[0m[1;35mprintf_common[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid*, char [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconst*, __va_list_tag*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m--___interceptor_vfprintf` indicates this is a format [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring-related issue in printf family functions.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Areas to Investigate:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Investigation Area**: [0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m726[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength_remaining > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m727[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mnext_tvb = [0m[1;35mtvb_new_subset_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m728[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m729[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mhave_tap_listener[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_follow_tap[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m730[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mtap_queue_packet[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_follow_tap, pinfo, next_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m731[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m732[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m733[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mcall_data_dissector[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_tvb, pinfo, tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m734[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m735[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m736[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have identified the root[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause and complete vulnerability chain:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function contains a **format string vulnerability** at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m where user-controlled packet data is used as a format string in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The vulnerability chain is:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m**: Raw packet data is read into `vis_packeth_raw_data` buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout proper validation or null-termination[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m**: This untrusted data is embedded into `d_output_buffer` via [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`snprintf` with `%s` format specifier[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m705[0m[39m**: `d_output_buffer` is used as a format string in `fprintf`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing format specifiers in the packet data to be interpreted[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Additional Critical Issues[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Wrong offset calculation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m663[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m664[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset++, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes but only increments offset by [0m[1;36m1[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No TVB bounds checking**: No validation that sufficient packet data exists [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore reading[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No null-termination**: Buffer not null-terminated after copying packet data[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Unsafe strlen usage** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m704[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Using `strlen` on potentially [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnon-null-terminated buffer[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Violates Wireshark standards**: Dissectors should not use fprintf/printf for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminal output[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Context from Comparison[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The v22 and v23 dissectors do NOT have any raw_data processing or fprintf calls[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No header field is registered for raw_data in the protocol registration[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This code appears to be debug/experimental code that was left in production[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `tools/checkAPIs.pl` explicitly lists `printf` as a restricted API for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissectors[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Recommended Solution: Complete Removal of Raw Data Processing[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Remove all raw_data related code from `dissect_bat_vis_v24` function** to make it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistent with v22/v23 implementations and eliminate all vulnerabilities.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove Variable Declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m648[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m653[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDelete the following lines from the function:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m646[0m[39m: `int [0m[33mvis_packeth_raw_data_size[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m647[0m[39m: `char vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m648[0m[39m: `char d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m653[0m[39m: `d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix Offset Initialization and Remove Raw Data Reading [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m659[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m659[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m with the correct offset initialization pattern from v23:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change line [0m[1;36m659[0m[39m from `offset = [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;` to `offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmatching v22/v23 pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove lines [0m[1;36m660[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m671[0m[39m entirely [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe incorrect offset++ pattern and raw data [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading loop[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace with proper field reading at correct offsets:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```c[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  vis_packeth->version = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  vis_packeth->gw_class = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  vis_packeth->tq_max = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove Format String Vulnerability Code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDelete the following lines:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m687[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39md_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[32m"B.A.T.M.A.N. Vis, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mraw_data %s"[0m[39m, vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m704[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m705[0m[39m: The entire if statement and fprintf call[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Add Proper Offset Calculation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m702[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd after the protocol tree items [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m702[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m* Calculate offset even when we got no tree *[0m[35m/[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset = VIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis matches the pattern in v22 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m488[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and v23 [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m609[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissectors.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Fix Protocol Tree Items Offset References [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m691[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m692[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince we're changing the offset initialization, the `proto_tree_add_ipv4` call at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m691[0m[39m needs updating. However, looking at the structure, after adding proper [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset calculation at VIS_PACKET_V23_SIZE [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, line [0m[1;36m691[0m[39m should work correctly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas it reads the next IPv4 field from that position.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is Optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Complete vulnerability elimination**: Removes format string vulnerability and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall related issues[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistency with existing code**: Makes v24 identical in structure to v22/v23 [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissectors[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Standards compliance**: Removes forbidden fprintf/printf usage from dissector[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No functionality loss**: The raw_data field has no registered header field and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserves no protocol dissection purpose[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Minimal risk**: Following proven patterns from v22/v23 that are already [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworking correctly[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All standard VIS protocol fields remain dissected [0m[1;39m([0m[39msender_ip, version, gw_class, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtq_max[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Protocol tree construction unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexcept removal of debug code[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Column info unchanged[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tap queue handling unchanged  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remaining data processing loop unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m711[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m734[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses All Issues:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. ✅ Eliminates format string vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprimary issue[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. ✅ Fixes offset calculation errors[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. ✅ Removes bounds checking issues[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. ✅ Removes null-termination issues[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. ✅ Removes unsafe strlen usage[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. ✅ Makes v24 consistent with v22/v23[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected - the removed code was debug/experimental code not part of the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard protocol specification[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
